The National Science Foundation (NSF) isthe lead support agency. Other sponsors\ninclude the Defense Advanced Research ProjectsAgency (DARPA), the National Aeronautics and\nSpace Administration (NASA), the Department\nEnergy (DOE).\n\nPURPOSE\n\nCENTER\n\no[ Commerce\n\n(DOC),\n\nand\n\nthe Department\n\nof\n\nThe JTEC assessments contributeto more balanced technology transferbetween Japan and the\nUnited States. The Japanese excel at acquisitionand perfection of foreign technologies,but the\nU.S. has relatively little experience\nwith this process. As the Japanese\nbecome leaders in research\nin targeted technologies, it is essential that the United States have access to the results.\n]\'I\'EC\nprovides\nthe essential first step in this process by alerting\nU.S. researchers\nto Japanese\naccomplishments.\nThe JTEC Endings cart also be helpful in formulating Governmental\nresearch and\ntrade policies.\n\nAPPROACH\n\nThe assessments are performed\nmembers are leading authorities\n\nby panels of about six U.S technical experts in each area. Panel\nin the field, technically active, and knowledgeable\nabout Japanese\n\nand U.S. research programs.\nEach panelist spends about one month of effort reviewing literatui=e,\nmaking assessments, and writing reports on a pan-time basis over a nine-month period.\nMost\npanels conduct extensive tours of Japanese laboratories.\nTo balance perspectives,\npanelists are\nselected from industry, academia, and government.\nThe focus of the assessments\n\nis on the status and long-term\n\ndirection\n\nof Japanese\n\nR&D efforts\n\nrelative to those in the United States.\nOther important\naspects include\nthe evolution\nof the\ntechnology, key Japanese researchers and R&D organizations,\nand funding sources. informal proceedings\nfrom seminars and conferences in the japanese research community,\nresults from recent technical\ncommittee meetings on Japanese national R&D projects, and contacts at R&D 011\'30\n\nGamota\n\nJTEC\nHIGH\n\nPANEL\n\nDEFINITION\n\nREPORT\nSYSTEMS\n\nON\nIN\n\nJAPAN\n\nAbstract\n\nThe\nsuccessful\nimplementation\nof a strategy\nto produce\nhigh-definition\nsystems\nwithin\nthe Japanese\neconomy\nwill favorably\naffect\nthe fundamental competitiveness\nof Japan\nrelative\nto the rest\nof the world.\nThe\ndevelopment\nof an infrastructure\nnecessary\nto support\nhigh-definition\nproducts\nand\nsystems\nin that\ncountry\ninvolves\nmajor\ncommitments\nof engineering\nresources,\nplants\nand\nequipment,\neducational\nprograms\nand\nfunding.\nThe results\nof these\nefforts\nappear\nto affect\nvirtually\nevery\naspect\nof the Japanese\nindustrial\ncomplex.\nThe\npresent\nreport\nrepresents\nthe\nresults\nof assessments\nof the current\nprogress\nof Japan\ntoward\nthe development\nof high-definition\nproducts\nand\nsystems.\nThe\nassessments\nare\nbased\non the\nfindings\nof a panel\nof U.S.\nexperts\nmade\nup of individuals\nfrom\nU.S.\nacademia\nand\nindustry,\nand\nderived\nfrom\na study\nof the\nJapanese\nliterature\ncombined\nwith\nvisits\nto the primary\nrelevant\nindustrial\nlaboratories\nand\ndevelopment\nagencies\nin Japan.\nSpecific\ncoverage\nincludes\nan evaluation\nof progress\nin R&D for high-definition\nsignal\nprocessing\nin Japan;\nhigh-definition\ntelevision\n(HDTV)\ndisplays\nthat\nare\nevolving\nin Japan;\nhigh-definition\nstandards\nand\nequipment\ndevelopment;\nJapanese\nintentions\nfor the use of HDTV;\neconomic\nevaluation\nof Japan\'s\npublic\npolicy\ninitiatives\nin support\nof high-definition\nsystems;\nmanagement\nanalysis\nof Japan\'s\nstrategy\nof leverage\nwith\nrespect\nto Elk\'us, Jr.\n\nPut eyes in the back of your\nhead. A navigation\nsystern in front\nof your nose. A telephone\nand fax\nin the middle of everything.\nA map pinpointing\ntraffic jams flashes\nacross your car\'s video monitor. Another monitor shows you right, left and\nrear views. All this as well as a voice\ncommand\nphone and mobile fax are but\na few of the advanced electronic\nsystems that Matsushita\nElectric is working on today, to make driving\nsafer,\neasier and more convenient\ntomorrow.\n\nYou\'re late for work, heading toward a traffic\njam and there\'s nothing you can do about it.\nha the future, this may not be a problem because\nof the advanced automotive electronic systems\nunder development at Matsushita.\n\nwith video cameras and monitors. And a unique\nHead-Up Display located in your line of sight\nwill show you speed, fluid levels and a map. So\nyou should never have to take your eves off\nthe road.\nTHE COMMUNICATIONS\n\nCENTER\n\nTo make your time on the road more productive,\nMatsushita is developing a mobile fax that will\nconnect your car to your office, home and beyond. A voice command mobile phone lets you\ncall anyone by simply saying his name out loud.\nIn any pre-programmed\nlanguage. And linked\nwith Matsushita\'s home automation technology.\nthe sound of your voice will lock or unlock the\ntYont door of your home. turn on the microwave\noven or turn on your air conditioner. All from\nyour car.\nHUMAN ELECTRONICS\n\nVISUAL INFORMATION\n\nSYSTEM\n\nShould you take the highway or the boulevard?\nOr maybe the back roads? Someday, your car\'s\nnavigation system will take care of all that. A\nnavigation map will show you traffic jams on a\nsophisticated video screen and show you exactly\nwhere you are. So you can choose the fastest,\nmost efficient alternate route.\nToday, you glance down to see the speedometer, up for the rear view mirror, left and right\nfor side views. Matsushita is working on a system that will replace side and rear view mirrors\n\nAdvanced electronic systems like these are an\nexample of how Matsushita Electric is de,,oted to\nthe concept of Human Electronics. Matsushita\'s\nobjective is to research, develop and market\nproducts that make life richer, safer and more\ncomfortable. These products are sold under the\nbrand names Panasonic. Technics. Quasar and\nNational. In 1988. Matsushita\'s\nconsolidated\nsales volume surpassed $41.7 billion. All a direct\nresult of a single-minded\nphilosophy:\nDon\'t\ncreate ne,a technology for technology\'s sake. but\nfor man", \';ake.\n\nMATSUSHITAELECTRIC\nPANASONIC TECHNICS QUASAR NATIONAL\n\nFigure 6.4.\n\n"Put Eyes in the Back of\'Your Head"\n\n180\n\nHigh\n\n::\n\nIt\n\n:\n\nhas\n\nsaid\n\nindustry\n\nHowever,\n\nDefinition\n\nTV\n\nhas\n\nvast\n\nrange\n\naddition\n\nto\n\nof other\n\nPresented\nbroadcasting\nrelated\n\nareas\nin\n\nthis\nstudio\n\nequipment\n\nfrom\nits\n\nthe\n\nTV\n\nof Leverage\n\nwould\n\ndominated\n\nversatility\nfor\n\ncreate\n\na\n\nprimarily\n\nutilizing\n\nhome\n\nTV\n\nof picture\n\nby\n\ncolor\n\nHigh\n\nDefinition\n\nbillion\n\nthe\n\nTV\n\nreceiver\n\nprocessing\n\nexcellent\n\n25\n\nunits.\n\ntechnology\n\nreproduction,\n\nHigh\n\npossibilities.\n\npossibilities\n\nmovies,\n\nfor\n\nprinting,\n\nwhere\n\na high\n\ncorner\n\nis\n\nsystem,\n\npubiishing,\ndegree\n\nas\n\nto\n\nStrategy\n\n:7\n\nfuture,\n\nendless\n\nThe\n\nDefinition\n\ncapability\n\nof\n\nvideo;\n\nSystems:\n\nprincipally\n\nbenefiting\nof\n\n:=\n\nHigh\nthe\n\nmarket\n\nvirtue\n\nhost\n\nthat\nin\n\nby\n\nThe\n\nand\n\n57\n\nbroadcasting\n\nand\n\nProducts\n\n:\n\nbeen\n\ndollar\n\nDefinition\n\nbe\n\nan\n\nused\n\nmedical\n\nof artistic\n\nexample\n\nwell\n\nas\n\nsamples\n\nin\n\nsome\n\nof\n\n6.B.\n\nHigh\n\nDefinition\n\n\'IV Studio\n\na\n\nand\n\nin\na\n\nis required.\nHigh\n\nof\nits\n\ninclude,\n\ntreatment,\n\nskill\n\nof\n\napplication.\n\nFigure\n\nTV\n\nHigh\n\npossible\n\nDefinition\nDefinition\nfields\n\nof\n\nmct.,_d J.
